<th>Misc. Notes
</th>
<td>Original images:&#160;ca.350dpi, color jp2&#160;files&#160;approx.&#160;2300 by 3500 usable&#160;pixels. Editing: re-sampled to 600dpi, converted to black and white tif files, de-skewed, and set uniform margins. Blank and title pages inserted to facilitate duplex printing. Disregard the Peachnote viewer that probably still shows color images. Removed title pages from individual parts and only parts that had music with a page number on the 2nd page had title pages, the title pages are not needed for those. PDF split of Cypressdome's "Complete Parts" file (#289894) by Sallen112.

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>Voices, Chorus, Orchestra
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>According to at least one source, a review by Philip Hale in the <i>Musical Courier</i> dated February 7, 1894, the work was orchestrated by Chadwick's student <a href="/wiki/Category:Hosmer,_Lucius" title="Category:Hosmer, Lucius">Lucius Hosmer</a> (1870-1935)
</td></tr></table>
</div>
